overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = it->second.to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Combine dense and overflow values\n    // full_value = (overflow << 4) | dense\n    uint64_t full_value = dense_bucket_.size();\n  double result = CONSTANT * m * m / harmonic_mean;\n\n  // Round to nearest integer\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(result + 0.5);\n}\n\ntemplate class
